The First Special District Court Strictly Handles Bribery Cases

突如其來千元鈔票　沈鴻舉發檢察處偵查 179

The case of Daxing Company suing Youcheng Company for the return of real estate and compensation for damages, which was accepted by the Shanghai First Special District Local Court, was handled by Judge Shen Hong. It had been tried twice and was scheduled to be pronounced on the 25th of this month. Unexpectedly, at 11:30 a.m. on the 22nd, while Judge Shen was working in the court, two people claiming to be surnamed Li and Gu sent a letter to Judge Shen's residence, stating that they wanted to see Mrs. Shen. After Mrs. Shen came out to meet them, they handed over the letter and left immediately, without being asked where they came from. The letter stated "To Mr. Shen Hong for receipt", and was signed "Respectfully from Ni Yunlai, representative of Daxing Company", containing banknotes worth 1,000 yuan, along with a note. Mrs. Shen was bewildered and immediately called Judge Shen to inquire. It happened that Judge Shen was busy with official business. He returned home from work in the afternoon and learned about it. He was deeply astonished and immediately reported to President Guo of the court. President Guo believed that the parties involved in the lawsuit dared to bribe the judge, which was a blatant disregard for the law. He handed over the original letter and the 1,000 yuan to the procuratorate for strict investigation according to the law. It is reported that arrest warrants have been issued and arrests are underway.

Yunfei Motors Mobilizes Entire Fleet to Search for Kidnapped Chinese Manager

盛燮圭昨晨在環龍路口被綁　公司汽車四出訪尋絶無踪影 180

Yesterday morning at around 8 o'clock, a kidnapping case occurred near the intersection of Avenue du President Haig and Rue Massenet in the French Concession. The victim was Sheng Xie Gui, a Ningbo native and the Chinese General Manager of Yunfei Motors, and Vice President of the Shanghai Rental Car Industry Association. When the news spread, all the cars of Yunfei Motors' head office and branches, as well as all the police cars in the Chinese and French concessions, were mobilized to search for the bandits' car, but as of late at night, there was still no trace of it. The details are recorded below:

昕夕辛勤 181

Yunfei Rental Motors Company in this city is one of the leading car rental companies in Shanghai. In addition to the head office located on Avenue du President Haig in the French Concession, there are nine branches in Pudong, Punan, and other places, with a total of nearly 200 cars. The Chinese General Manager of the head office is Sheng Xiegui, a Ningbo native. Sheng is 46 years old and has been working for the company for many years. Because he is usually capable in his work and diligent, he has gradually risen from a small staff member to his current position. Sheng is responsible for the management of the Chinese part of the company. Yunfei's success today is largely due to Sheng's efforts. Because he is trusted by the people, he was also elected as the Vice President of the Shanghai Rental Car Industry Association.

突遇綁匪 182

Sheng's home is located at 124-126 Avenue du President Haig near Rue Massenet, close to Yunfei's head office. At 8:50 yesterday morning, after Sheng finished breakfast, he went to the office as usual. He walked out of his residence alone and proceeded along Avenue du President Haig across Rue Massenet. When he arrived near the Avenue Haig Villas, he suddenly saw a young man in a suit holding a newspaper, leaning against the wall and silently reciting. When Sheng approached him, the young man suddenly drew a gun, forbade him from making a sound, and forced Sheng back to the corner of Avenue Massenet and Avenue du President Haig. A green Chevrolet bandit car was parked there in advance, with four bandits lying in the car.

面色慘白 183

At that time, the four bandits in the car saw that the victim was already in their hands, so they all drew their guns and forced Sheng into the car. One bandit drove, and drove straight into Avenue du President Haig, turned west, and sped past the entrance of Yunfei's head office. At that time, an old storekeeper named A Long was working in the company and had been serving in the company for many years. He was very alert. He happened to be returning to the company and unintentionally caught a glimpse of Sheng, his face pale, being held in the car by five unfamiliar young men in suits, heading west. A Long knew something was wrong and rushed to report to the company. A Westerner manager heard the news and immediately called the French Concession Police Station, the various police stations in the Public Concession, and the district offices of the Public Security Bureau to request a pursuit.

家庭情况 184

The manager then ordered all Yunfei branches to mobilize all their vehicles to search for the bandits' car. For a time, police cars and Yunfei cars were all over the city, but as of the afternoon, there was still no trace of them. It is reported that Sheng has been working for Yunfei for nearly 20 years. In addition to his wife, he has two sons and a daughter. The eldest son, Zhonghan, is 18 years old and is studying at Chengzhong Middle School on Tangshan Road. The second son, Xinghan, and the young daughter, Yuanyuan, are still young. Sheng's younger brother has passed away, and his brother's wife, nephews, and nieces all rely on Sheng alone for their livelihood. This kidnapping has led to speculation that the purpose is not money but something else special.

光華汽油跌價 185

The Great American Evening News reported that the wholesale price of Guanghua Company's gasoline has been reduced to 8.2 cents per gallon, and the retail price has also been reduced to 9.5 cents per gallon. The gasoline prices of other companies have not yet fallen in competition.

浴佛節將屆　靜安寺前又聚商成市 186

Guowen News Agency reported that April 8th of the lunar calendar, commonly known as the Bathing Buddha Festival, is the date when the annual fair is held in front of the Jing'an Temple on Jing'an Temple Road in this city. Along both sides of the road, various vendors set up temporary shops, which is what the villagers call catching the fair. During this period, not only do tourists gather from all directions, but also the incense of Jing'an Temple is continuous day and night. Most vendors earn several months' worth of food at this fair. Last year, the Municipal Council banned the fair because it hindered traffic, but this year, after villagers requested it, it is still being held as usual. Yesterday, although the festival had not yet arrived, temporary sheds had been erected along the road, as dense as combs. Furniture made of rattan, bamboo, and wood was piled up into a market. People walking in it felt as if they were hundreds of miles away from Shanghai. The incense pilgrims and sightseers in Jing'an Temple were already extremely crowded yesterday. The police temporarily dispatched Indian mounted police and foreign police to patrol back and forth. This custom has been going on for many years. In the past, villagers would go to Jing'an Temple to burn incense during the Bathing Buddha Festival and come to sell the goods they had made throughout the year. Gradually, some stayed permanently and only returned to their villages after the fair was over. The monks in charge of Jing'an Temple collected rent from this, and the income was used for charitable causes, such as providing medical care in the summer and school expenses. This has become a custom, and the annual gathering has been unchanged until now.

永安同人公讌新監督 187

The Supervisor of Wing On Company was originally filled by Guo Le, and the Director was Guo Biao, the General Manager was Yang Huiting, and the Deputy Manager was Guo Lingshuang. Last year, Guo Biao passed away, and the vacant position was unfilled. This year, Yang Huiting also retired due to old age. The company felt that there were shortcomings in the responsible person's work. It is reported that the board of directors has decided to appoint Guo Shun, the General Manager of Wing On Textile Company, as the Supervisor, as he is familiar with commercial affairs and capable. Guo Lingshuang was promoted to General Manager, and Guo Le's son, Guo Yuewen, was promoted to Deputy Manager. The colleagues of the company felt that they had found the right person, and yesterday, important staff representatives of the colleagues held a public banquet at the Dadong Restaurant to express their congratulations. At two o'clock, the toasts were exchanged, and it was a grand occasion.

滬西發見四五十盜匪 188

大刦工作塲

A Westerner named Jiang Sen of Meihua Real Estate Company purchased several acres of land on the side of Zhongshan Road near Hongqiao Road in western Shanghai and built three tall and magnificent residential villas. Construction has been underway for several months, and the project is now 60% complete and is being rushed to completion. Unexpectedly, at about 1:10 a.m. yesterday morning, a large number of bandits, 40 to 50 people, armed with eight or nine handguns and two wooden-cased guns, broke through the bamboo fence from the south and rushed in. They first fired two shots into the sky to intimidate, then five bandits guarded the night watchman Pan Ciyuan, and more than ten bandits guarded the masons Gu Amao and Zhang Asan next to the site. The remaining bandits then searched and looted. After about an hour, more than 300 pieces of five-cent plywood, about 500 feet of white lead water pipes, and more than 40 pieces of silk and cloth clothing belonging to the workers were looted. After carrying away the stolen goods, the bandits still fled south. When the leader of the Criminal Investigation Team of Western Shanghai, Xia Pinshan, and Deputy Leader Tang Bingxiang received the report, they immediately led the detectives to pursue them, but the bandits had already fled far away. After inspecting the scene, they found 37 pieces of the original stolen plywood abandoned by the bandits on Zhongshan Road, about a mile away. Subsequently, the Westerner Jiang Sen of the company opened a list and reported to the Sixth District Police Station, requesting a strict crackdown on the stolen goods and bandits.

建屋領照華探索賄敗露 189

Ch'u Shao-ch'ing, a building contractor, submitted an application to the French Municipal Council on February 24th of this year, requesting a permit to build the Nanhua Banquet Hall and Guohua Cinema (buildings) at the corner of Avenue Edward VII and Rue Grosse (i.e., Songshan Road). After the Municipal Council forwarded the application to the French General Police Station, the Investigation Team of the Seventh Group sent Chinese Detective Cai A-san, also known as Xiao Maogou, No. 119, to investigate. After reporting back to the Western supervisor, on March 12th and 13th, Detective Cai was ordered to summon Ch'u to the police station's office. When the group leader questioned him about the construction situation, Cai took the opportunity to demand a reward of 500 yuan from Ch'u, saying that it could expedite the issuance of the license. Now, Ch'u reported the information to the police station. Upon receiving the report, the police chief believed that Cai dared to solicit rewards from people, which was a dereliction of duty. He dismissed Cai from his position, ordered him to be detained, and yesterday, he was transferred to the Second Special District Court for prosecution. At 3:30 in the afternoon, Criminal Judge Wang Gangxu presided over Criminal Court One for interrogation. First, police lawyer Fei Xizhen stated the case, indicting him according to Article 128 of the Criminal Law. Then, the plaintiff stated the circumstances of the case. When the defendant Cai A-san was questioned, he denied soliciting rewards from the plaintiff and hired lawyers Zhu Dianqing and Ge Zhizhen to defend him. According to the witness, translator Jin Miaoquan, he testified in court that he had heard the defendant and the plaintiff talking about money in the writing room, but he did not understand what kind of money it was. After examining the confessions, the court ordered a change of date for further interrogation. The defendant was ordered to provide a surety who could be summoned at any time to await further instructions.

嚴諤聲捐贈工部局圖書館 190

丨中文書籍三千八百卷丨

The Shanghai Municipal Council's Public Library has never had many Chinese books. 少年以頭抵壁地上血漬斑斑

以小洋刀自刎原因始終未明 191

The Shanghai Tobacco Exchange Association is located at No. 487 Zhongwang Lane, Ningbo Road, in the Public Concession. The upper floor is rented to the family members of the owner of Xin Changtai Company. Yesterday afternoon at about 12:15, the maid employed by Xin Changtai Company was carrying the tableware down from the upper floor, intending to wash it by the tap, when she suddenly saw a young man wearing a long gown standing face to face with the wall at the back door of the house, not leaving for a long time. The maid felt very strange, so she walked out of the back door to investigate and saw that the young man was pressing his head against the wall, with bloodstains all over the ground. She pushed him, but he did not move or respond, only shaking his head slightly. The maid was terrified and rushed upstairs to report everything to the owner and told the people in the Tobacco Exchange Association to come out and see what was going on. The people in the association ran out of Zhongwang Lane and reported to the nearby police station at No. 1713 to come and see. It was then discovered that the young man's throat had been cut with a knife, and he was still holding a small foreign knife tightly in his hand. The police urgently hired a car to take him to Dehe Hospital for treatment. It is reported that the injuries were very serious and his life may be in danger. It was later learned that the young man's surname was Li, his name was Bochao, he was from Dongyang, Zhejiang, and he had studied at the China Public School. It is still difficult to guess why he had such a sudden intention. We must wait until he recovers before we can ask him what happened.

Publishing World 197

▲Mr. Wang Jin's "On Chinese Criminal Law" Mr. Wang Shuping, since the early years of the Republic of China, studied in Japan and has been intensely passionate about criminal law. He personally learned from famous Japanese scholars, grasping their essence and principles. After returning to China, he lectured at various universities in Peiping, offering unique interpretations, referencing new theories, and providing comparative evaluations of the merits and demerits of Chinese criminal law. In addition to his lectures, he authored "On Chinese Criminal Law," a book of over a thousand pages, totaling more than fifty thousand words. This monumental work is unmatched in its time. Soon after publication, readers rushed to purchase it. Consequently, the first volume has been printed seven times in just a few years, while the middle and lower volumes have reached their fourth edition. The entire set of three volumes is priced at four yuan, six jiao, and two fen. Now, as a special offer to readers, a discounted price of 20% off is being offered. It is reported that the books have already been shipped to Shanghai and are being sold on consignment at the Pei Wen Zhai Bookstore, located at the west end of Guangxi Road on Sanma Road.

▲Dawn's New Publication: Famous Works on Economics The Value Theory History, a famous work on economics recently published by the Dawn Bookstore on Simma Road in this city, is translated by Professor Sun Hanbing of Jida University. The content includes famous works such as the "History of English Value Theory" by the German scholar Lebkraus, the authoritative economist Rubin's "On Ricardo and the Basic Characteristics of General Classical Economic Theory," and Buharin's "On the Value Theory of the American School." Not only is the translation fluent, but also the original text is attached to each important point for reference. It is not only suitable as a university textbook, but also a must-read for economic researchers. It is said that the whole book has 500 pages and only sells for one yuan and eight jiao, which is also very cheap.

Incoming Mail

Shanghai Pudong Fellow Villagers Association's Declaration on Raising Funds to Purchase Land and Build a Clubhouse 202

Our Shanghai Pudong Fellow Villagers Association was founded in August of the 20th year of the Republic of China. At that time, there was a proposal to build a clubhouse, but it was not carried out because a suitable site for purchasing land had not been found. In recent months, we have found a site east of the intersection of Avenue Edward VII and Chengdu Road, with an area of nearly three mu. We have decided to raise funds to purchase it and build a clubhouse at the same time. Mr. Huang Yanpei wrote an article to inform our elders, brothers, sisters, and cousins from our hometown, saying that the national crisis is urgent. Why are we building this civil engineering project? We do not know that the construction of the clubhouse of our fellow villagers association is precisely to save the country from its crisis. China has a population of over 470 million, yet it has been repeatedly insulted by Japan, which has a population of less than 70 million. Over 3.87 million square miles of land have been occupied and cannot be recovered. More than 33 million people have been massacred and forced to be managed and cannot be rescued. Although there are many reasons for this, the main reason is the lack of unity. Now, if we really want to save China from its crisis, we must have principles and methods. One essential condition is that everyone must abandon their selfish and self-interested individual views, first form small groups, then combine several small groups into large groups, and then combine several large groups into one large national group. When the one large national group is formed, the foundation of the country will be established, the strength of the country will be strong, and the life of the country will be eternal. What is Japan? It is not worth following or mentioning. How do we start forming small groups? Human affection is most easily expressed in sincerity and love when people leave their hometowns. Therefore, the combination of natives in one place is often not as large and solid as the formation of a group of compatriots in a foreign land based on the relationship of "fellow travelers in a foreign land." Shanghai is the transportation center of East Asia, and this example is particularly evident. Looking at the city's population of 3.84 million, how much strength can be shown, and what group of fellow villagers is considered important at one time? All are non-native groups. Taking a step further, observing several non-native groups, which one can be considered more powerful? We know that the answer will be unanimous and without hesitation: Ningbo people, Ningbo people! Ningbo people are also Chinese citizens. Is it that they are naturally endowed with a particularly strong and solid unity? There must be a reason for this. In the second year of the Jiaqing reign of the Qing Dynasty (1797 AD), the leaders of the Ningbo people who were merchants and workers in Shanghai initiated a proposal, and the masses responded below, creating the Siming Public Hall. Over time, the scale gradually expanded, and the benefits to their fellow villagers became increasingly complete. When they first came to Shanghai, they were provided with accommodation. When they were sick, they were provided with medical care. When they died, they were provided with burial. With the relationship of relatives, friends, neighbors, and fellow villagers, they were introduced to jobs. They celebrated each other's happy events and offered condolences. They helped each other and showed compassion in times of trouble. What people seek from the group is only to live in peace and enjoy their lives. With such a group, how can it not become a gathering in one year, a village in two years, and a city in three years? Twenty years ago, the Ningbo people established the Ningbo Fellow Villagers Association, and soon a great building was completed, providing education for those seeking knowledge. The Siming Public Hall was mostly for the working class, while this was mostly for the intellectual class. Since the opening of Shanghai as a port, the Ningbo people have held the reins. Now the number of people has increased to one million, accounting for almost one-third of the city's population. In the 13th year of the Tongzhi reign (1874) and the 24th year of the Guangxu reign (1898), when their tombs were encroached upon for road construction, the masses resisted one after another. In a weak country, they ultimately made the Westerners yield. Any group that can gather strength to treat its members well like this will inevitably become strong and large. Is it only the Ningbo people who are like this? If the Ningbo fellow villagers did not have a vast site of tens of acres, facing the Republic of China Road, crossing the Baliqiao Road, and west of Mintiniyin Road, and a magnificent building of tens of feet high towering on Xizang Road, without this organization, the cause would not be so broad, the people would not be so numerous, and the unity would not be so solid. The Ningbo fellow villagers took the lead, and all those who wanted to strengthen and enlarge their groups followed suit, encouraging and striving forward, dividing into powerful public groups in one direction, and uniting into a whole organic body, using it for self-reliance and to face the outside world. The direct and indirect impact on the survival and development of the country and the nation is unlimited. Our Pudong fellow villagers deeply believe in the irrefutable theory and the powerful precedent, and gather to discuss and plan to make a concerted effort to gather all sectors of knowledge and labor, and on the selected site, combine the strength of the group to build the great building of the future. We have hired fellow villagers who are skilled in architectural design to design it carefully and in detail. It will have several floors, several rooms, several halls, and several halls. The land and house will cost about 400,000 yuan in total. It was decided that those who donate more than one hundred yuan will have their names inscribed, those who donate more than one thousand yuan will have their portraits hung on the wall, those who donate enough five thousand yuan will have a room named after them, those who donate enough ten thousand yuan will have a hall named after them, and those who donate more than thirty thousand yuan will have a hall named after them. At this point in the discussion, Mr. Du Yuesheng rolled up his sleeves and said, "Please allow me to donate the most money for the hall," doubling the amount offered. Everyone responded enthusiastically, saying, "Wonderful! Please build the largest hall in the center with Mr. Du's donation and name it Du Hall, to celebrate Mr. Du's birthday. The largest hall is named Du Hall, and the hometown pronunciation of 'large' is similar to 'Du'." In the future, when people pass by Avenue Edward VII and see the magnificent building with old and young men and women entering and exiting by the thousands, they will be settled when they first arrive, educated when they seek knowledge, introduced when they seek employment, and provided with medical care when they are sick. They will celebrate each other's happy events and offer condolences. They will help each other and show compassion in times of trouble. In peacetime, they will meet and talk and hold meetings. In their leisure time, they will be entertained. Listen to the dialect they speak, all of which are Pudong hometown sounds. Without looking up to see the plaque, they will already know that it is the Pudong Fellow Villagers Association. The public and private affairs of the Pudong people are developing day by day, and their contribution to society and the country is becoming more and more great. The foundation of the country will be established, the strength of the country will be strong, and the life of the country will be eternal. From then on, there will be no more national crises. All of this is the gift of Mr. Du and our elders, brothers, sisters, and cousins from our hometown. Mr. Huang Yanpei recalled that at that time, he was ordered to write the article and actually carried out the task of the devil, and he was also honored to participate in it, and he would not dare to be selfish. April of the 20th year of the Republic of China, Huang Yanpei.

Reader Consultant 203

A collection of letters discussing the question of (Can one go back to the countryside?) (19) A letter from Mr. Liu Zhaomin of this city丨A reply to Mr. Zhu Tianqing Today I read Mr. Zhu Tianqing's letter in this column, saying that he "found that I was showing off my writing to irritate people," and also said that I "occupied the space of the reader consultant for nothing." Regarding the latter, I want to apologize to the readers of this column, and I feel really uneasy. As for this letter replying to Mr. Zhu Tianqing, I didn't want to write it anymore, because I was afraid that my "unskilled in rhetoric" and "specially fond of showing off" writing would "irritate" Mr. Zhu, and no one would go to the countryside to build a "new paradise" in the future! However, I cannot avoid this suspicion of "specially showing off writing to irritate people" and give up my right to discuss. Moreover, Mr. You's qualifications as a "leading figure" who feels the pain of the countryside, the first is "literate and able to write." I criticize your writing with the construction of words, but I have offended you. Let's not talk about that, let's ask for Mr. Zhu's teachings again. (1) "The most important thing about the suffering of Chinese farmers is that they have no knowledge." The most powerful part of Mr. Zhu's sentence is the word "indeed." In fact, there is no such easy thing. Mr. Zhu, this sentence fully expresses your demeanor of chatting "sitting comfortably on the sofa," and you don't know the suffering of the farmers at all. This doesn't require you to talk about theory, nor does it require the ability to "read and write," let alone rhetoric. As long as you are willing to give up your blessings and go to the bankrupt and vast countryside for a trip, tell the farmers that you have no knowledge, and you are very painful, and you have no education, and you are very painful. If the farmers don't treat you as a madman, then I will lose. But if you want to ask them, do you feel painful if you don't have food to eat? The farmers will definitely answer immediately, of course. The current pain of the farmers is really not a question of whether they know knowledge or not, or whether they are educated or not, but that the whole family is hungry, and their wives, children, old and young are crying for food. This is a common fact in the Chinese countryside. You need to know that Mr. You's advice to people to return to the countryside is not only theoretically untenable, but his method is also completely based on his ignorance of the real situation in the countryside. Although there are chickens and eggs in the countryside, the current "chickens and 'eggs'" are different from those decades ago. A chicken sold to the city can get more than one yuan, and an egg sells for sixty or seventy yuan. They are reluctant to eat it themselves and want to exchange it for money to buy seeds and pay off debts. They only eat sweet potatoes, beet sugar, and flour. Where can they get "reading chickens" or "thirty eggs" or "one yuan" to give you? Moreover, the children in the countryside (we are naturally talking about the poor tenant farmers and hired farmers) have to go to graze cattle, collect manure, and pick up firewood for their families when they are seven or eight years old. They even have to be sent to the rich farmers' homes to graze cattle in exchange for a bowl of rice to eat. Where can they have the leisure to let their children read this unlucky book and receive this unlucky education that cannot be eaten when they are hungry and cannot be clothed when they are cold? Moreover, you already know that "the reason why rural education in China is not developed is because 'politics is not on track, warlords are fighting internally, communists are disturbing everywhere, foreign capitalist forces are invading, and there are excessive taxes, etc. These frequently cause great blows to the countryside and make farmers and the countryside bankrupt. Almost all poor farmers are too busy to take care of themselves, so how can they take care of rural education?'" You should work hard on these reasons, which is the right thing to do. Why don't you talk about the real problems of these reasons head-on, but talk about rural education in mid-air? Under the current situation of what you call "politics not on track, warlords fighting internally..." etc., what practical and broad significance and effect can there be in using rural education to treat the head when it hurts and the foot when it hurts?

Free Talk

Besides Jade Legs and Creamy Bosoms 204

— Xuan

During the January 28th Incident, Shanghai's cinemas were truly closed for several days. Later, after the "bedside agreement" was signed, "forgetting entertainment while saving the country," or "saving the country while not forgetting entertainment," the cinemas resumed their former prosperity.

However, films that specialize in "jade legs and creamy bosoms" have been heavily criticized! Because these lewd and sensual films can wear away the ambition to resist Japan and save the country.

At the same time, martial arts and superstitious films have also been criticized! Because these feudal-minded films can numb people's minds.

At the same time, the saying that movies are a sharp weapon for mass education has been shouted even louder. For a time, everyone was demanding films that promote national spirit, films that promote domestic products, or films that promote hard work in production. Film companies were also busy changing direction. Although it came late, after the first anniversary of the January 28th Incident, we finally saw these brand-new films such as "Torrent," "Night in the City," and "Three Modern Women." It is said that these films can indeed compete with imported "jade legs and creamy bosoms." But right now we are in the "War of Resistance Against Japan." The people should have the determination to "resist to the end." The people should know how the soldiers on the front line are "fighting bloody battles" and quickly and enthusiastically transport supplies. Naturally, there is still not enough with only "Torrent" and so on! Naturally, we must produce several "War of Resistance Against Japan" films!

This is a consistent demand from top to bottom! And those above are already preparing.

However, we have seen several scenes of the "War of Resistance Against Japan." The most unforgettable of these is the escape of General Tang Yulin. This is not a "refreshing" program, so it is unlikely to be adopted. Then, what will be adopted is probably the victory at Xifengkou, the bravery of the Big Sword Team, with a magnificent name such as "Give Me Back My Rivers and Mountains." In this way, the people will know that they have indeed "resisted" and will not forget "give me back," and they will naturally be extremely grateful!

This is opening up new paths other than "jade legs and creamy bosoms" and "martial arts and superstition," which is enough to make the people put down one hundred and twenty-four hearts and wait drunkenly for the final victory of the "long-term resistance"!

What to do when returning to the countryside? 205

— Yang Xingzhi

丨Reply to Mr. Cao Juren

The other day, I published an article entitled "Returning to the Countryside and Eating Meat Paste" in this magazine. The main purpose of this article is to point out that the proposition of returning to the countryside to create a "Shangri-La" is not only a Utopian dream, but also a smoke screen containing a strong anesthetic and deceptive nature. Because it cleverly plants a beautiful hope in the minds of the masses, it pulls the masses away from reality, and it shifts the goals of the masses to another illusion. Of course, we should "firmly oppose" such a proposition of returning to the countryside.

However, due to space limitations, I only said half of what I wanted to say in the previous article. In fact, I am also in favor of returning to the countryside, because people who are unemployed and cannot live in the city, have no A-brand sterilized milk to eat, and have no possibility of drinking, playing mahjong, or filling in "liberation lyrics," can "damn the national affairs," but their own affairs cannot be "damned." If they want to "manage," they have to return to the countryside. There are many things in the countryside waiting for us to start, and many partners are waving to us. Naturally, we should return to the countryside to find a "way out." Just squeezing in the city is just waiting to die, just "escaping." I was planning to write another article to supplement the unfinished meaning of the previous article. It just so happened that Mr. Cao Juren first came up with a "biased defense of returning to the countryside" and expressed "dissent" to my previous article. I think this disagreement is very meaningful.

However, I am still not satisfied with Mr. Cao's disagreement. On the contrary, I still want to express "firm opposition." Because Mr. Cao's proposition of returning to the countryside is just a new annotation to the previous proposition, and the mistakes made are no different from the former, and such "amelioration theory" may be more vicious in its effect than the former. Whether Mr. Cao's proposition is out of "consciousness" or not, the resulting errors are the same.

Why? First, Mr. Cao divides the current Chinese countryside into three types, A, B, and C, and believes that returning to type C countryside "will never be disappointed." This is a huge mistake. Because he stubbornly divides the "entire" capitalist world, the "entire" colony, and the entire collapsing countryside into three types of regions that are not connected and seem to be able to "exist independently," and ignores the reasons for the current collapse of the countryside and its trends. He seems to believe that the soil in the upper reaches of the Qiantang River is a "blessed land" that is "free from exploitative relations," "unaffected by political and economic factors," and "will never collapse," which can accommodate all the unemployed and build a "kingdom" of self-cultivating farmers. But is this really the case? This is Mr. Cao's mistake one.

Second, Mr. Cao seems to believe that "self-cultivating farmer economy" is the most ideal solution to the land problem and the most satisfactory destination for the peasant problem. This kind of "recognition" may inevitably be a serious mistake, and he excludes many agricultural proletarians from the circle and advocates "organizing self-cultivating farmers alone to fight a self-defense war" to resist the erosion of capitalist economy and the sucking of corrupt local bullies to maintain this "blessed land." This is especially a big mistake. Furthermore, Mr. Cao's self-defense method is "to help self-cultivating farmers form a strong national system to collectively farm in order to realize agricultural electrification, so that self-cultivating farmers can keep their own land and their own machinery." In these few words, there are plans, organizations, struggles, industrial revolutions, agricultural revolutions, and perhaps an independent regime. It is great, but can this great project be undertaken by thousands or tens of thousands of "self-cultivating farmers" in the upper reaches of the Qiantang River? This is Mr. Cao's mistake two.

Third, Mr. Cao said: "Let's see the efforts made by consumer cooperatives in the progress of the Soviet revolution." That's right, consumer cooperatives have indeed played a considerable role in the Soviet revolution - no, in the construction process of the Soviet socialist economy. However, that is only in the "Soviet Union!" Oranges will become trifoliate oranges when they cross the Huai River. The Five-Year Plan cannot be implemented by any country! This is Mr. Cao's mistake three.

With these three mistakes, Mr. Cao's "disagreement" is still just a smoke screen, an illusion.

However, in the end, I still advocate "returning to the countryside," because there are many partners in the countryside waving to us, and there are many things waiting for us to start.

Bitter Smiles, Groans, and Cries 206

— Ba Jin

丨To My Brother丨 (Continued)

You have returned to the North. In these past eight years, we haven't been together for even a month in total. Now, I am about to embark on a life of wandering. It seems that there will be no more time for us to gather quietly in my hopes. Last night, at a friend's house, I told you: I want to find an opportunity to stake my young life on a single throw. I want to do something exhilarating, even if it means destroying my entire life without hesitation. You didn't say anything at the time; you just smiled slightly.

Perhaps you wouldn't understand this situation. "Why should you abandon the writing life?" In your mind, this question cannot be answered. But in fact, you know that I haven't written anything for three whole months. I would rather spend my time on the streets, in trains, and at friends' houses, wasting my young life. But the opportunity I hoped for never appeared, and people outside are saying in articles, as if shooting arrows in the dark, that I am already lamenting that my pen is about to run dry.

Of course, you wouldn't believe such rumors. We have spent nearly twenty years of life together; you know how faithfully I have experienced all of this. My beliefs, my character—you know them very well. I have never finished writing what I wanted to write, and I have never let the mist cloud my eyes. I am still alive now, not lying down, yet people are using all kinds of rumors to bury me. I have never uttered a protest against these rumors. I only have bitter smiles; I only have groans.

These groans, these bitter smiles, are piling up on my shoulders. For two years, they have piled up so high, and now they leave such a long shadow behind me. I am gradually beginning to hate my name. At first, I said I loved my writing, but now that my writing has been ruined enough by others, I also hate my writing. I am still struggling in the darkness, my eyes looking towards the unreachable light ahead, and my writing is almost suffocating me, my name is almost destroying my faith, my character. Today, I can no longer smile bitterly; I can no longer groan. I say all of this should end.

When I first dedicated myself to writing, I was full of faith; I was full of hope. I regarded writing as a part of my life, and I walked the path of writing with a faithful attitude. I was determined: I would not become a literati. You know that I have always hated literati. We often said that we shouldn't become literati in the future because literati are either direct plunderers or tools of plunderers. We were accustomed to seeing the ugliness of literati in our childhood. Who knew that cruel fate would actually cause me to be regarded as a literati today, and everything we hated has been added to me. Rumors, exploitation, manipulation, attacks, flattery—for the past two years, they have surrounded me, surrounding me so tightly that I cannot breathe a breath of free air. There was a time when I even suspected that I was about to enter the grave.

Under these circumstances, I wrote my "Cry of the Soul." That article was written last autumn when we met in Tianjin, in your colleague's small room. After it was published in a certain magazine in Shanghai, a friend who I had never met read it and shed tears of pity, saying that he didn't expect my life to be so painful.

In that article, I said that I wanted to end my literary life. But after I returned from the North, my life fell into more rumors, exploitation, manipulation, attacks, and flattery. These insults, accompanied by illness, pressed me down so that I couldn't move. I lay in bed for several days, and I thought about my life before I wrote novels. I thought about the few teachers I admired in life, and my heart was tormented by regret. A voice rang in my ears: "You can live like this again. You should stand up and be a brave person!"

That's right, I am too weak! As a "writing person," I am indeed too weak! For the past two years, I have let all insults be added to me, and I have never uttered a protest. I have smiled bitterly and groaned too many times. I traveled the so-called Chinese literary world with a child-like innocent heart. I believed in everyone, and I loved all my friends. And then all kinds of things happened that made me smile bitterly and groan: "To be continued"

Carrot Top 207

— Jules Renard, Translated by Lin Qu

Chamber Pot (Two)

He woke up suddenly, listening to his stomach.

"Ah! Ah! This is bad!" he said.

He thought he had gotten away with it. He had been too lucky. He really shouldn't have been lazy last night. Now the punishment is really about to come.

He sat on the bed, pondering. The door had already been locked from the outside with a key. The windows were barred. It was impossible to get out. Yet he still got up and felt the door and the bars on the window. He crawled on the ground, reaching under the bed with his hand, searching for the chamber pot that he knew very well wasn't there.

He lay down and got up again. He would rather move, walk, and stamp his feet than lie down. He rubbed his swollen stomach with both fists.

"Mama! Mama!" he called softly, afraid that others would hear. Because if Mrs. Lepic came, she would immediately say that nothing was wrong and that he was deliberately joking with her. He called like this only so that he could say tomorrow without a guilty conscience that he had called her.

And how could he shout loudly? All his strength was used to make the disaster happen a little slower.

Before long, a very severe pain made Carrot Top dance. He leaned tightly against the wall and then jumped away. He leaned tightly against the bed rail. He leaned tightly against the chair. He leaned tightly against the fireplace. He violently pulled open the iron plate in front of the fireplace. He squatted down, curled up in a ball. He surrendered. He was suddenly extremely happy.

The room was even darker.

Chamber Pot (Three)

Carrot Top didn't fall asleep again until dawn. In the morning, Mrs. Lepic seemed to smell something outside and came in with a strange face, pushing open the door, while he was still not up.

"What a strange smell!" she said.

"Good morning, Mama!" Carrot Top said.

Mrs. Lepic pulled off the sheets, sniffing all over the room, and found it in a short time.

"I felt unwell last night, and there was no chamber pot in the room," Carrot Top said quickly, thinking that this was the best way to defend himself.

"Liar! Liar!" Mrs. Lepic said.

She ran out, secretly brought in a chamber pot, and quickly stuffed it under the bed. She dragged Carrot Top up, called everyone in the family, and shouted:

"What sins have I committed to have such a child?"

She sometimes brought rags and a bucket of water, as if putting out a fire, and flooded the entire fireplace. She shook the bedding and called for air! Let in air! Busy and complaining.

She sometimes pointed at Carrot Top's nose and said:

"Damn thing! Have you lost your senses! You're acting abnormally! You're acting like an animal! We give a chamber pot to an animal, and it knows how to use it. But you, you want to roll in the ashes of the fireplace. God knows, you've made me confused. I'm going crazy, crazy, crazy!"

Carrot Top, barefoot and wearing a nightgown, stared at the chamber pot. There was no chamber pot last night, but now there was a chamber pot under the bed. This empty, clean chamber pot made him dizzy. If he insisted on pretending not to see it, that would be too insensible.

His family had already made a mess, and some neighbors with mocking expressions, as well as the postman who delivered the correspondence, all joked with him and asked him many questions.

"I swear to you!" Carrot Top finally replied, looking at the chamber pot. "I, I'm simply baffled. Do whatever you want with me."

Education News

Second Shanghai Municipal Inter-School Sports Meet Opened Yesterday 208

▲ More than 4,000 male and female athletes from 66 schools participating

▲ More than 20,000 spectators, sports continue this afternoon

The Second Municipal Inter-School Sports Meet, organized by the Shanghai Municipal Bureau of Education, officially opened at the China Athletic Field on Rue du Père Huc yesterday afternoon. Mayor Wu Tiecheng, the president of the meet, personally attended and delivered the opening speech. A grand parade and mass exercises were held. More than sixty schools participated, with more than four thousand athletes and students participating in the mass exercises. The weather was fine, the wind was gentle, and the entire field was crowded with people, with colorful flags waving and cheers thundering, creating a magnificent scene. Visitors flocked in, and the streets around Rue du Père Huc were jammed with traffic. The sports competitions were orderly and neat. The staff served enthusiastically, and the athletes were full of spirit. The order in the venue was slightly lacking in discipline. The track and field events were all preliminary and semi-final rounds, and the results were acceptable. The field events were all finals. There were seven events for men and women in total. Today's program is even more important than yesterday's, and it is expected to be even more interesting. The grand occasion of yesterday is recorded as follows:

Grand Opening

A Glimpse Before the Opening 209

At 1:00 PM, under the warm sunshine, the China Athletic Field was filled with enthusiastic people. Colorful flags fluttered across the field, dazzling the eyes. The loudspeaker first announced the gathering of male and female students from various schools in order to assemble in the center of the track and field, quietly awaiting the mass exercises. The male and female athletes were lined up on the track. The audience was densely packed around the field, impenetrable. At that time, the heads of ten thousand people were moving, and the voices were boiling. How magnificent! How magnificent!

Circumambulating the Venue 210

After the athletes and mass exercise students were arranged, the parade began. It started from in front of the main platform. The Shanghai Municipal Police Bureau military band led the way, followed by the staff of the meet, and then the male and female athletes from various schools, who were estimated to occupy three-quarters of the 400-meter track, marching forward to the beat. The sound of footsteps and music were mixed together, and the atmosphere was solemn and magnificent.

President Delivers Opening Speech 211

After the parade was over, they reassembled in front of the main platform and performed the opening ceremony. After the ceremony, President Wu Tiecheng delivered the opening speech in a clear, concise, impassioned, and extremely pleasing tone. The general idea was that holding sports meets every year is to examine our bright strength, and this bright strength is sufficient to maintain the survival of the country and our lives.

President and Mayor Tiecheng Delivers Opening Speech (Photo by Xu Tianzhang) 212

And we want to use it to resist our enemies and achieve the goal of recovering lost territory. Physical education is the foundation of all kinds of undertakings. The survival of the country and the nation depends on the bright strength to resist our opponents, and the creation of this strength depends entirely on you young people. The annual sports meet is to test how our usual training is.

Vice President Pan Reports 213

After Lin Meiyan, the representative of the Municipal Party Headquarters, delivered a training speech, Vice President Pan Gongzhan reported, (1) This sports meet is the Second Shanghai Municipal Inter-School Sports Meet. The first one was held at the end of April two years ago. It was suspended last year due to the Shanghai War. This session will be held for three days starting today. (2) This conference has expanded its scope. All schools established in this city and private and provincial middle schools approved to be established may also participate. As a result, 66 schools participated in today's conference, including 5 municipal schools, 59 private schools, and 2 provincial schools. In terms of gender, there are 55 male schools and 11 female schools. (3) The conference focuses on track and field competitions, dividing into eight trophies for male and female A and B groups, teams and individuals. Sports schools compete separately. Thousands of students participate in track and field events, and more than 2,000 participate in mass exercises. Including group performances, there are more than 4,000 people in total. The feature of this conference is the addition of mass exercises for more than 2,000 people and various group exercise performances. (4) The conference has obtained the lease of the venue from the China National Sports Association, the promotion of the municipal government, the assistance of various bureaus, the support of sports people, and the publicity of various newspapers, so that this grand sports meet can be held.

Singing the Sports Meet Song Together 214

At the end, the sports meet song was sung. This song was composed by the musician Chong Zhitong, who also came to the venue to guide. First, the Police Bureau military band played it once, and then the mass exercise students sang along to the beat. The lyrics were produced and printed in 10,000 copies by the Shanghai Diligent Bookstore Sports Editorial Department and distributed to the audience at the venue.

The Situation During Mass Exercises 215

After the singing was over, the mass exercises were held. As many as sixty schools participated in the mass exercises. Shao Rugan broadcast slogans on the loudspeaker, and Dong Chengkang demonstrated. The movements were neat and orderly. The opening ceremony ended here. Then the competition began immediately.

▲ Medals and Scoring Methods The conference set up eight medals, team boys A and B, girls A and B, and individual boys A and B, girls A and B. The scoring method is to take the top four in each event, with 5, 3, 2, and 1 points respectively. The first place gets 5 points, the second place gets 3 points, and so on. Relay races are also divided into male and female A and B groups, taking the top four places with 16, 4, 2, and 1 points respectively.

Individuals with excellent results will also be rewarded separately. The scoring method is the same as that of middle schools. Overview of Field Events 219

Cheng and Zhong competed for the result, Cheng was third and Zhong was fourth.

Girls Group A Long Jump Wu Meixian came after being eliminated in the 100-meter race and took the best result with 4.18 meters. In the last three jumps, she improved to 4.26 meters. (2) Dai Pu improved from 3.77 meters to 3.95 meters. (3) Lu Meiyun improved from 3.67 meters to 3.80 meters. (4) Chen Liuzhen got 3.79 meters, only 0.01 meters away from Lu Meiyun. ▲ Men's Physical High Jump There were only five people in total. Zhang Jiakui of Jiangnan won first place with 1.585 meters. The other four were from Dongya. The results of the second, third, and fourth were all equal, so they rolled back to determine the order of points.

Track Race Report 220

▲ Wu Meixian Fined Twice Ms. Wu Meixian is one of the four heroines of the former Harbin, and has attended national and Far Eastern sports meets. She is a well-known figure in the sports world. Ms. Wu is currently studying at Fudan Practical Middle School, so she was able to show her skills at yesterday's Municipal Middle School Sports Meet. She is the most hopeful female player, but yesterday she was fined for two false starts in the 50-meter race, which was a pity for those who heard about it. Then she hoped to see her skills again in the 100-meter preliminary, but unexpectedly she was fined for two false starts again, which can be said to be extremely unfortunate. According to Chen Bingde, the instructor of Fudan, Wu's false start was actually because she usually practiced without listening to the instructor, so she had today's result. If so, then yesterday's fine is enough to be a lesson for Ms. Wu.

▲ Training for High Hurdles Lacking In the preliminary of the men's group A high hurdles, no one in the four groups had a good performance. The mediocrity of the results is not to be mentioned. Their running posture is not good, and the steps are not accurate, so many hurdles fell, and the results were not good. It is actually because of the lack of training. Among the track races, this sport can be said to be the least interesting.

▲ Kite Flying Suffers Greatly One hundred people participated in the 1500-meter men's A preliminary, which is the highest record in Shanghai's sports meets. Each group of 25 people in each of the four groups only takes three places, which can be said to be difficult. Watching each preliminary, inexperienced players like to fly kites, that is, after the starting gun is fired, they exhaust their life's strength and rush forward to show off and belittle others. However, the process is long and the strength is insufficient. The glory of the moment is difficult to maintain for a long time. Before a lap is over, they are exhausted and fall to Sun Mountain, and even withdraw halfway. It is very appropriate to call it a five-minute fever. They really don't know how to use their strength.

▲ Comparison of Women's 100-Meter Results After Ms. Wu Meixian was fined for a false start in the women's 100-meter A and B groups, no good results appeared. The best one also needs 15 seconds, which is Xiao Jieying of Wuben. In the second group, there were originally five people in the race, and three people were fined for false starts. Only two people competed, and they were completely admitted, taking advantage of the cheapness. The result was 16.6 seconds. This is called taking advantage of the cheapness. Also, there are no good results in the women's physical education school.

▲ 50-Meter Kung Fu Is Not Bad The results of the women's A and B groups in the 50-meter race were not outstanding, but in the women's physical education school group, Chen Wanqing and Sheng Bi of Dongya are not bad at kung fu. The former is 7.4 seconds, and the latter is 7.5 seconds. It is expected that there will be more to see in today's final. Sun Zheng and Ren Song, two ladies from the Southeast, have excellent sprinting at the end. Their posture is wonderful at the finish line, which is very kung fu. It can be said that they have been deeply trained.

▲ Men's 100-Meter Race Has a Fierce Battle In the men's 100-meter race, the talents are quite average. Although the results are not good, the situation is very tight. Liu Jiaxian of Minli, Li Songnian of Daxia, Lin Shihua of Fudan, Dong Yinchu of Guanghua, Cheng Zhonghong of Fudan, and Guan Changfa of Nanfang have similar kung fu. There will be a fierce battle in the final.

A Glimpse of the Venue 228

▲Announcing a Full House: The three stands—east, west, and north—were packed with spectators, with no room to spare. Latecomers had to stand in front of the fences. The effort was naturally unquantifiable. Among the spectators, there were many large groups of male and female students in neat, uniform school uniforms. From a distance, they were quite a sight to behold. There were likely over 20,000 people in the audience.

▲Magnificent Parade: The athletes from each school first made a parade around the track. After the military band came the staff, then the female athletes, followed by the male athletes. Due to the large number of schools and people, the military band had already returned to the front of the podium before the back started moving. The 400-meter track was almost insufficient to accommodate them. During the review, the school flags of each school were lined up, fluttering in the wind. The variety of colors was already quite striking. And the two thousand plus male and female students, following the loud slogans, moved in unison, which was extremely spectacular.

▲Sound Film: The Shanghai office of the American Fox Film Corporation was in charge of filming the event with sound. Among the photography technicians were Chinese photography expert Wang Xiaoting and several Westerners, moving east and west, extremely busy. It is said that the most exciting two to three hundred feet of footage will be selected and sent to New York, and then returned to Shanghai for public release, sometime after March.

▲Order Issues: The order at the venue was generally very good. However, some Boy Scouts lacked experience in maintaining order, leading to outsiders being found in the venue from time to time. The 200-meter finish line lacked a fence, so people leaked in. This was a common occurrence. It is hoped that more capable Boy Scouts can be deployed.

▲Boy Scout Service: Commander Wang Gang, Leng Xueqiao; Deputy Commanders Xie Yanbo, Yu Julu; Dispatch Chief Jiang Yin Seng; Group Commanders and Coaches of various group divisions. The Boy Scouts serving at the venue: Junyi 30, Dongya 50, Guangzhao 50, Tongyi 20, Kaiming 50, Wudao 20, Shangzhong 50, Yousheng 20, Fudan 20, totaling 310.

Sideline Stories from the Venue 232

▲Many Temporary Booths Outside the Venue

Around the conference venue, in addition to the mat sheds built by the conference for male and female athletes to rest, there were also many temporary cloth sheds built by various schools. They surrounded the venue, connected to each other. Statistics showed that there were four from Guangzhao Public School, one from Qinghua Middle School, one from Minli Middle School, two from Shanghai Middle School, three from Guanghua Middle School, one from Daxia Affiliated High School, three from Xing Shi Middle School, three from Dongya Sports College, one from Southeast Women's Sports College, one from China Women's Sports College, and one from Kaiming Middle School. The Boy Scouts from Guangzhao Public School and Kaiming Middle School even camped at the venue.

▲Women's Military Review Faster Than Men's

During the general military review of each school, the broadcasting station repeatedly called for the movements to be slower. During the first section of the exercise (slapping hands upward while circling the arms), over four thousand strong arms were seen continuously waving, just like waves churning in the sea. The girls standing in the south moved faster, so it looked like the waves started in the south and fell to the north.

▲Famous Athletes as Spectators

This citywide middle school joint sports meet was of great concern to famous sports figures in Shanghai. Those who came to the venue as spectators on this day included Xiao Dinghua, former Northeast University student who held the national high hurdles record; Dong Jiaxie of Tongji University, who held the East China 1500-meter record; and Sun Huipai, a long jump champion from Shanghai. In addition, many veterans from the Baihong Jiangnan track and field team also came to visit, watching the emerging athletes compete on the field, all eager to give it a try.

▲Two Peddlers Were Dragged Away

Before the 400-meter preliminary for Group B, two peddlers somehow entered the venue, carrying baskets filled with peeled water chestnuts, preparing to make a speculative business deal. Coincidentally, a Western-dressed staff member in the conference saw them, went up, and unceremoniously dragged them out of the sports venue, eliciting different reactions from the spectators.

▲Three Generals Temporarily Become Actors

Ms. Huang Jingzong from Wuben Girls' High School, Ms. Qian Xing Su from Dongya, and Ms. Chen Baixue from Liangjiang, these three generals, in the preliminaries, each won first place. So, a certain Western film company hired them to be on camera and simultaneously captured their delicate voices. Ms. Huang said, "I am very happy today and wanted to run first, and I did run first." Ms. Qian said, "I ran the 50 meters today and came in first. I am very happy and hope to run first next time." Ms. Chen said, "I am very happy to jump first today."

▲The 400 Meters Are Evenly Matched

Wu Yougang, a rising star from Qingxin, has spent several years in school diligently practicing pole vaulting and the 400-meter run. Sure enough, yesterday's result was only five-tenths of a second behind General Guan. He is expected to perform even better in today's 400-meter final. This is expected. Another rising star in middle-distance running, Ji Songen, also had a remarkable result. It is also hoped that he will work harder today to create a new record.

▲Watching One Set After Another

During each school's group exercises, each school showed their specialties, and tens of thousands of people watched with rapt attention, getting carried away, and singing the Jiangbei tune in their mouths ("Watching one set after another, wonderful, wonderful!").

News

The United Association of Middle School Teachers Will Petition Today for Aid to Various Schools in the French Concession That Have Been Closed 235

The United Association of Teachers and Staff of Secondary Schools in this city has been greatly outraged to hear that the authorities of the French Concession have illegally forced the Morning Light Girls' Middle School and other schools to suspend classes. They believe that this move hinders our country's educational administrative power. Therefore, they have resolved to send representatives to petition the party and government yesterday. However, because yesterday happened to be the opening day of the city's Middle School Joint Sports Meeting, all the leaders of various agencies attended to participate, so it was temporarily decided to change it to this morning to carry their petition separately to the party and government, requesting serious negotiations with the authorities of the French Concession to achieve the goal of resuming classes.

Wang Shijie to Take Office as Minister of Education Around Early May 236

The newly appointed Minister of Education, Wang Shijie, was previously urged by former Minister of Education Zhu to send a telegram, and he replied in a telegram stating that he would come to Beijing as soon as the affairs of Wuhan University were settled. Recently, it was heard from a friend in Beijing who had corresponded with Wang that Wang's wife had gone to Nanchang and has now returned to Wuhan. The period for sorting out the affairs of Wuhan University and coming to Beijing to take office is around May 1.

The Ministry of Education Implements Education to Influence and Transform Red Areas 237

(Nanjing, 27th) The Central Executive Committee believes that the Red Bandits use communist heresies to bewitch the people, forcibly indoctrinate youths and children, establish Red schools everywhere, compile Red textbooks, and anesthetize the children in the bandit areas. Therefore, it has formulated special measures for the implementation of education in special areas and a special training program for primary schools, which have been issued by the Ministry of Education to order all areas that have been disturbed by the Red Bandits or are currently deeply Red-infected to comply with.

The Chinese Education Association Sends a Telegram to Party, Government, and Military Leaders in Various Places, Urging Unity Against Foreign Aggression 238

▲Planning for an Important Meeting in Beijing in the Near Future

▲Quickly Organize the Troops to Go to the Front Lines Together

The United Association of Teachers and Staff of Secondary Schools in Shanghai, in view of the increasing foreign disasters and the increasingly dangerous national situation, sent a special telegram yesterday to the party, government, and military leaders in various places, urging them to unite to resist foreign aggression and save the country. The original telegram is as follows: (Titles omitted) Since September 18, the violent Japanese have displayed their power, occupied our Northeast, disturbed our Shanghai, and recently have been pressing forward step by step, peeking at our Beijing-Tianjin area, attempting to occupy the hinterland. At a time when disasters are deepening, the Communist bandits in Jiangxi are also taking the opportunity to stir up trouble, directly restricting the central army and indirectly helping the violent Japanese. Internal and external troubles are approaching each other. If all of us Chinese people cannot bear to sit and wait for death, we should rise up together to save the country from danger. This association believes that the current way to save the country is to fight against Japan and suppress the bandits at the same time. In order to complete these two great and difficult tasks, it depends on the sages and heroes of the party and the country, the military and political leaders, to be of one heart and one mind, and to unite in sincerity. Unexpectedly, in the past year or so, the party leaders have not shown understanding of the national crisis. A few politicians are even competing for private opinions all day long. Central University is fighting hard on the front lines, while the Southwest has been talking about sending troops, but not a single soldier has been dispatched to the front. Now the situation is urgent. The members of this association, recalling the daily shrinking territory and the imminent demise of the nation, thinking of our isolated army in the front, resisting the fierce bandits with flesh and blood, especially express their views and earnestly hope that the party, government, and military leaders in various places will adhere to the principle of unity in good faith, concentrate their opinions, and go to Beijing in the near future to plan for a major plan to save the country. It is especially hoped that the soldiers in various places will fulfill their duties, quickly organize the troops, and go to the front lines together. Hesitation and observation will bring disaster to the party and the country. Consistency in words and deeds can save this crisis. National survival and national revival depend on this one action. The telegram is urgent. I hope you will consider it. 'Shanghai United Association of Teachers and Staff of Secondary Schools, bowed. (Rest)
