Spring and Autumn

Stupid? 245

— Baihe

Not many days ago, all the newspapers in Shanghai published a news item from a certain foreign news agency, roughly saying that at the home of a certain Russian woman in Harbin, while the Russian woman was not at home, not only did thieves steal all her belongings, but they even stole the entire house, leaving not a single tile behind. When the newspapers published this news, they all used the headline "Stupid Thieves".

This kind of unprecedented theft does indeed seem a bit incomprehensible. What things are not worth stealing? Is there really nothing more valuable than these broken tiles and leftover bricks that is worth stealing? But upon closer thought, I feel that the words "stupid thieves" are still not entirely certain.

In the interior, there are petty criminals who "hit with a club" and "carry the mother-in-law", and heroic figures who demand "leave the money to buy the road", specifically targeting the "lone geese" who travel alone, who are easier to deal with. If you kowtow like pounding garlic, you can still keep your head and not worry about food. If you have learned three days of Tai Chi, "one five-jin is very six-jin", and if you don't eat "wonton", you will definitely eat "broad noodles". This kind of behavior, under the pen of a gentle friend, is called "murder and robbery". After "murder and robbery", if you don't do it, you don't stop, and then you come up with "destroying the corpse and eliminating traces" to eliminate the root of the disaster. If stealing things includes stealing houses, then they are "stupid thieves". Then, "destroying the corpse and eliminating traces" should be stupid thieves. Before the "September 18th Incident", all our sovereign rights in the Northeast had already been greatly occupied by Japan. This is just like "a hero encountering a 'lone goose'", "what's yours is mine". The "lone goose" leaves the money to buy the road in the "hero's" pocket himself. But the "hero" doesn't do it once, and he doesn't stop. He not only robs, but also kills. After killing, he also destroys the corpse and eliminates traces, covering the entire Northeast land with interwoven Japanese flags and puppet flags. Although the old man insisted on leaving the Wang land without sovereignty to China, the "hero" was still "deaf as a donkey to the spring breeze", going straight ahead to the end.

What is the difference between stealing things and wanting houses, and seizing sovereignty and wanting land?

The Power of the Masses 246

— Sisu

Japanese soldiers are really formidable. No matter how strongly Song Zheyuan and Shang Zhen resist, given a month or so, the counties of eastern Hebei will eventually follow in the footsteps of Liaoning, Jilin, Heilongjiang, and Rehe. The people of the country may inevitably be shocked and discouraged, thinking that unless the Japanese soldiers do not attack, they will win if they attack, and China cannot resist them. In fact, that is not entirely true. China also has a sure-win weapon, but it is a pity that the people of the country do not use it! This weapon is boycotting Japanese goods. When the people of the country see the four words "boycott Japanese goods", they inevitably think it is an old cliché, nothing new; but the power of this boycott is really very great!

There was a Japanese-run "Shuntian Times" in Beiping, which can be regarded as the pioneer of cultural aggression. Its circulation was very large, said to be about 100,000 copies. This was not for anything else, but because the newspaper was unscrupulous and could say anything. For example, in the era when Zhang Zuolin was the Grand Marshal and the Northern Expeditionary Army resisted, the newspapers run by the Chinese all avoided talking about defeats and spoke of victories. Grand Marshal Zhang had many taboos, and even Mei Lanfang's performance of "Feng Huan Chao" almost caused a fatal disaster, saying that "Feng" was a homophone for "Fengtian," cursing that he could not stay in Beiping and had to return to his old nest in Fengtian, which could be compared to the prohibition of performing "Da Gu Ma Cao" during Cao Kun's reign. However, the "Shuntian Times" did not buy Grand Marshal Zhang's account, reported the truth, and the people of Beiping knew the truth about the front line, and everyone bought it to read. Grand Marshal Zhang could not do anything about it. Who knew that the Jinan Incident caused a boycott. First, the newspapers run by the Chinese advised people in editorials to boycott the "Shuntian Times" and awaken national consciousness. Everyone's emotions surged, and they stopped buying it. Moreover, Chinese stores could not stop stopping advertising, economic panic occurred, they could not support it, and they announced a suspension of publication. The power of the masses is so great. If all the people of the country insist on not selling or buying Japanese goods, the entire Japanese economy will panic to the point of being unable to support itself, just like the "Shuntian Times", and will naturally collapse. The Chinese have this sure-win weapon, but they put it aside and only expect military victory. Isn't it a pity!

School Life Cartoon 247

— Zeng Shujuan

During math class, it's everyone's time to secretly read novels; things like "Sexual History", "Flying Catkins", "A Bundle of Love Letters", ... are all good reading materials during this hour. Although it's sneaky and secretive, it's still more lively and interesting than boring math!

The toilet often displays "wall literature" by general unknown writers. If you observe carefully, it's just as numerous as "slogans" when the revolutionary army sets out. Things like "Down with the useless professor!" "Down with the 囗囗 fat man!" are all "good materials" here!

Everyone scrambles to grab the Saturday newspaper; they are not looking at any news, nor are they reading any commentary. What they urgently want to know is: what movie is playing at a certain cinema tonight? And what drama is playing at a certain theater tonight?

A half-length portrait of a Western-suited gentleman and a small scarlet envelope written in red ink are often placed under a female student's pillow. After dinner, people strolling leisurely on the playground, in twos and threes, talking and laughing, are either sworn sisters or fellow villagers with close ties.

The director of student affairs can be said to be the "target of public criticism" for the students. Often, a strange, fashionable young man, once he becomes the director of student affairs, will soon be given a string of "nicknames", even though he never jokes with the students.

Selling Children 248

— Zhou Jingzhi

The faint sunlight shone through my window curtain from the diagonally crossing trees on the pavement. It was only seven o'clock, and it was a fine Sunday! I was in a gentle village, pursuing a good dream, when suddenly a series of tragic cries woke me from my spring dream.

"Selling children! Boys are eighteen yuan, girls are eight yuan." A man and a woman, resembling a couple, were sitting by the street; the tragic voice came from the haggard woman's mouth.

Ah! The bustling city, the intoxicating city, I can't believe there is such a contradictory fact. Men are eighteen yuan, women are eight yuan, what a cheap price! However, as a student, I really have the feeling of being unable to help! Only staring at their pitiful shadows, and a series of sad voices stirred my soul.

X X X X X

"Selling children! Boys are eighteen yuan, girls are eight yuan."

"························"

From morning to noon, they shouted for several hours. From beginning to end, it was so memorable. I really don't believe that among the wealthy people, there wasn't a single compassionate person, letting them shout, except for a few coolies, expressing sympathy and sighing. This was seen as disappointment in their eyes, irrelevant.

The voice gradually became low and faint. The selling price of eighteen yuan and eight yuan had been reduced to twelve yuan and five yuan, but who would help them with the sad facts? And who would pity their situation and help them?

In the evening twilight, I watched their black shadows disappear faintly, but the sound of "selling children" still hovered in my mind.

The Bee's Sting 249

— Sha Fei

Passionate men are most likely to grab one love, then another, and another, so their happy beginning is the beginning of pain.

○ ○ ○

If you need to find a lover to break your loneliness, then after they leave, you will feel even more lonely.

○ ○ ○

There is no feast in the world that does not end. The failure and conclusion of love, although extremely painful on the soul, can be said to be supreme joy if it can be decisively cut off!

○ ○ ○

There are two kinds of conflicts between men and women. One kind is a valuable conflict that is not only easy to explain, but will also increase feelings. The other kind is a worthless conflict that often drives men and women to extremes, and the result is the destruction of feelings!

Long Novel

Northeast Fourth Company Commander 250

— Zhang Henshui

Chapter Five: Boiling Tea to Pass the Long Night, Sadly Remembering the Year's End, Inscribing Resistance to Violence, Shouting Loudly

Jiang Shi said: This is outrageous. No matter how civilized a person is, descendants and incense cannot be said to be unnecessary. Otherwise, everyone will not care, and where will the world still have people? Talking about this brought up infinite thoughts in Zhao Weng's mind. He was sober from the wine, and there were no more drunken words. He held an empty teacup in his hand and was just staring blankly. Seeing the pot of hot water placed on the iron stove, it was already boiling. Gurgling, white gas was coming out from the spout and the lid seams. Jiang Shi also saw that it was New Year's Eve, so she shouldn't make the old man sad, so she smiled and said, "Old man, you asked me to make dumplings. Is the dough ready?" Zhao Weng said: "The dough is ready, and the filling is also prepared, just lacking someone to wrap them." Jiang Shi said: "Let's not leave our hands idle while we talk here. My daughter and I can wrap them with you first." Zhao Weng was a restless person. After hearing this, he went to the kitchen himself and brought out a green tile basin of dough and a bowl of filling. So Jiang Shi and her daughter washed their hands and faces, and placed the dough and dumpling filling on a square stool, and wrapped them around the square stool. Zhao Weng took a rolling pin and placed it next to him, holding the dumplings they had wrapped. After a long time, he couldn't help but sigh and said: "Time really flies! I remember when I was little, on New Year's Eve, my mother and my sister were making dumplings, and I was watching by the side, wasn't it just this situation? In the blink of an eye, it has been fifty years." Guizhi said: "As the saying goes, muddling through the days, muddling through the days. No matter what, it's really fast once you muddle through. It takes us a lot of effort to boil a pot of water. Look, we casually put a pot of water on this iron stove, and it boils without us realizing it." These words reminded Zhao Weng, and he smiled and said: "If we don't make tea, the water will boil dry." So he poured three cups of tea and placed them on the table. Before he could distribute them, Guizhi took the pot to add cold water, brought the pot back, and placed it on the stove. First, she offered a cup to Grandpa Zhao, and then offered a cup to her mother. Zhao Weng held the teacup in one hand and stroked his beard in the other, and smiled at Guizhi: "This girl is very quick-witted. If I had one like this by my side, I would be much happier." Jiang Shi smiled and said: "Didn't I say? The old man dotes on her so much. She is a child without a father, so let her kowtow to the old man and become his goddaughter." (55)

Novel

Struggle 251

— Zhu Qingyun

(One)

The sky was so cold, in the storm of wind and rain, there were also snowflakes; in the gray and dim sky, they shot fiercely like chaotic arrows. The enemy's heavy artillery roared even more, as if it had gone mad, and the large-caliber shells flew one after another in the air. The terrifying explosions, carrying the splashing mud and trees, like water columns rolled up by a hurricane, splashed up one by one, in the fire of the shell explosions.

In the trenches of our army far away, the water was so deep that it had almost soaked the straw mats, making them almost float up. The cold power of the wind and snow, and the bombardment of heavy artillery, made the soldiers in my trenches surrounded by a tragic and dangerous environment. Although the weapons were unfavorable, they had boiling blood and heroic ambition, and they still lay in ambush and waited calmly. Although they watched the terrible shells fall on the trenches from time to time, and splashed the not very strong defensive works and the comrades who were resisting the enemy in the trenches together, they only had grief and indignation, only the heart to avenge, struggling with their flesh and blood bodies and the environment. The sound of artillery was scarce, and the chaotic and heavy footsteps, mixed with the sound of the charge bugles, rolled over in the north wind; that group of yellow-clothed dwarf soldiers, unevenly arranged, lined up in a battle line, like shadowy ghosts in the darkness, charging forward step by step. The enemy was getting closer and closer, and our army had received the order to meet them head-on with a heavy blow. The soldiers' accumulated grief and indignation were vented in a earth-shattering shout. After a burst of sweeping from the rattling machine guns and the booming hand grenades, the front row of dwarf soldiers had fallen like a mountain, but the endless enemies behind were rushing in like a tide; but our bullets were about to run out.

"Forward, fight!" One brother drew out the broadsword on his back, which was as white as snow, slightly tightened his body, and leaped out of the trench. "Good! Forward." Many soldiers drew out their broadswords one by one, jumped out of the trench, and waved the broadswords together, whistling like countless snowballs, rolling straight into the enemy's human tide.

The whistling of the knives, the banging of the guns, and the mournful screams mixed together. This is the struggle of flesh and blood and sharp weapons! 丨丨 The struggle for a faint trace of justice.

(Two)

The stores that have great sales all year round often find slogans such as "Intending to close, recouping the principal", and "Closing down sale, special sacrifice". The beginning of the year is so bad, ordinary stores are struggling to survive in the collapsing economy. The number of unemployed people in society is therefore increasing day by day.

Since the company he worked for was reorganized 丨 that is, sold 丨 he has been unemployed. Although he has asked people for help everywhere and entrusted people to introduce him, he has not been able to find a suitable job for five or six months. Although the expenses of the small family are minimized, in this era of rising living costs, five yuan for rent, about ten yuan for food, and social expenses, no matter how tightly you tighten, an expense of about twenty yuan cannot be reduced any further.

With great difficulty, he entrusted a relative and sent a resume, along with his usual manuscripts and writing style, and received the following reply: "Your matter has been handled by my brother to the best of my ability. Mr. So-and-so, the clerk in our office, has just been absent due to illness. If you are willing to take this position, please come to Shanghai to take up the job immediately. The salary is twenty yuan, without meals. However, in this autumn of overstaffing, there are many who seek such a hard job, so I have to hope that you will come early, lest others take the opportunity to occupy it: : :"

Twenty yuan, excluding meals, how much can you send home in Shanghai, where it is not easy to live? However, if you don't go, you can't even get this little money. If you go, it's still not enough for household expenses, but if you don't go, the great disaster in the future will be even more unthinkable. He thought, sighed, and discussed it with his wife, and decided to leave his hometown and take up this job that was not enough to live on.

The spring breeze was so chilly, and the climate was so cold, but the station was crowded with people struggling for life. He went on a journey, although he knew that the struggle for life was still in an unstable environment, but there was no second path besides moving forward and struggling. The struggle of flesh and blood and sharp weapons, the struggle of life and economy, wrote the epitome of modern China.

Ningbo Banks Mostly Roll Over Loans 256

According to the assessment of the silver and banking industries, the amount of long-term loans from Ningbo banks to Shanghai reaching maturity this time is no less than 10 million. In prosperous business times, there would be no need to recall these funds, but due to the numerous incidents this year, there are concerns about potential risks, so they have to undertake a partial small-scale closure. Unexpectedly, the matter went against their wishes, and most debtors requested rollovers due to their inability to repay. The Ningbo banks had no choice but to grant these requests. As a result, rollovers reached 8 to 9 million yesterday, and those not yet due will also be rolled over upon maturity. Furthermore, the interest rate has fallen by almost half a yuan compared to the last term (late last year). In addition, long-term deposits and withdrawals yesterday were also no less than 5 to 6 million, with interest rates ranging from 8.5 to 11.5 yuan, a difference of about 3 yuan.

The market price uniformly fell back slightly, with demobilization bonds falling by 7 jiao 5 fen. In reality, since the closing had already been canceled and today is the settlement stop for the April futures contract, most people were taking a wait-and-see approach, and the trend became uncertain. Silk and Tea 266

Linping

Poor Development of Silkworm Eggs in Zhejiang Province

In the nearby silkworm farming areas, farmers are limited by economics this year, and many are hatching local species. In addition, the weather is still cold, and there have been ten days of continuous rain, which is not suitable for the progress of silkworm rearing. Although all rely on fire for heat, development is not favorable. Silkworm eggs have occasional changes. Most of the early batches have been abandoned. Even the late silkworms that have been added still have slow silkworm development due to the sudden sunny and rainy weather. Currently, most of the early silkworms that have reached the third sleep and have enough leaves have stopped eating and are not sleeping, and many are suffering from softening disease. Late silkworms have just reached the second sleep and do not eat leaves vigorously. A bumper harvest is hopeless.

Xiaoshan

This term has been designated by the government as a model area. All categories are leading the rearing of improved species and have instructors to assist in the instructions, and also take over the progress of drying the green, etc. However, the weather is abnormal, and the development of silkworm eggs is quite slow. Early batches in Toupeng, Shanxin An, Shushan, Kan Shan, Wenyan and other places are still only three-sleep vigorous leaves. In Cangqian, Nansha, Xiaosibu and other places, late batches are only two-sleep full leaves. The weather is still cold these days, and most of the silkworms are shrinking and not sleeping. Early silkworms are not eating leaves vigorously. Although the temperature is adjusted with fire, it is still difficult to improve development.

No One Asks About Silk Cocoon Shops in Jiangsu Province 267

The Su-Zhe silkworm season is affected by the cold weather and continuous rain, which affects the development of silkworm eggs. Silk cocoon merchants in Shanghai are very discouraged about the silk cocoon collection problem. In addition, the financial community's loans are strict, so there is no preparation for departure to collect silk cocoons. In the silk cocoon shops in Jiangsu Province, this time of year was already booked, but this term no one asked. According to people in the silk cocoon industry, the silk cocoon market in Jiangsu Province will inevitably decline invisibly this term. Few silk cocoon shops have been rented out. In Wuxi County, there are 200 silk cocoon shops, except for 78 which have been rented by local silk cocoon merchants to prepare for weighing and collecting cocoons. The rest have no one to host. According to statistics, less than one-tenth of the silk cocoon shops in Jiangsu Province have been rented out this year, and most of them are contracted by each shop to collect and deliver cocoons.

Commentary

Voluntary National Salvation 273

— Tianfang

National salvation, it is said, is not a term that makes people turn up their noses and walk away. On the contrary, it is quite fashionable, such as "dancing for national salvation," "entertainment for national salvation," and "beauty for national salvation." Roughly speaking, the fact that the nation needs to be saved today is beyond doubt, but for us, who "establish the nation with writing," we are quite particular about "rites." Therefore, there is no room for discussion regarding the choice of words. This is because "if the name is not correct, then the words will not be smooth."

Recently, it was reported that a "Voluntary National Salvation Association" has been established in Guangdong Province. As the name suggests, it is known that it comes from the people and is not forced by the government. National salvation must come from "voluntary," which has the idea of "driving" oneself. Is it also out of necessity? However, it is dangerous!

Since the "September 18th Incident" when Japanese artillery fire bombarded China, the sound of "national salvation" has been overflowing in the country. But to whom does this responsibility ultimately belong? Is it the "political power" or the "administrative power"? Because there is no clear regulation, it is still not very clear. Some say that this is the responsibility of the people, but after the transformation from "long-term resistance" to "absolutely not speaking of resisting Japan," it seems to be a matter for a few people in high positions, and the common people have nothing to worry about. In short, there is no constitutional provision, as long as you do not "endanger the Republic of China," you can be considered a good citizen. Whether to save or not to save is quite free.

Perhaps saving without saving can save the safety of one's life and property. In this year when one cannot move, it is better to eat quietly and be more generous. It is also possible to regard artillery fire as fireworks or sound movies. After dinner, it is good to open the newspaper and read the good news. You do not need to ask where this good news comes from. Whether it is "resistance against Japan" or "suppression of bandits," you do not need to care about which country the people who are "temporarily headed" or "captured" belong to. In short, all good news is good. Now we have wise ministers internally and good generals externally, so we are not afraid of not being able to save the mere China. All of us common people, although it is said that there are "internal troubles and external threats," in reality, "we are not afraid." Therefore, in terms of reason, "national salvation" is "absolutely impossible." In terms of power, it is also unnecessary, so you can rest easy. If you think it is absolutely necessary, or you are afraid of being suspected of falling behind, then choose what you are close to, such as "dancing" and "smoking," and "go together, go together" is also possible. Just remember to follow in other people's footsteps and never act rashly. This is not your right. Otherwise, moving and making a conclusion contrary to the topic is not something to be happy about, but a little bit sad.

Literature and Art

The Bloody Battle of Xifengkou 274

— Zhou Gongmou

For a score of days, blood was shed to protect the endangered city,

Several times, machine guns swept the enemy camp,

I would rather break my head to prolong the national lifeline,

A real man is ashamed to flee for his life.

Loss of Each Pass of the Great Wall

The barbarian horses neighed wildly, shaking the old capital,

The stench of mutton permeated the ancient Great Wall,

Watching China be reduced to barbarians,

What is the reason for fighting and fighting in the wall?

Looking to the Southwest for Troops

The beacon fires lit up, and the barbarian drums urged,

Ten thousand miles of the country is handed over to the remnant ashes,

The south is broken to see the flags,

The mystery in the pot is very expensive to guess.

Singing the Treasured Sword

The light rises, the flames of the invaders, and the barbarian flute is urgent,

The generals and their swords in the box are angry and ming at times,

Wielding the horse to transform the dragon and run to the north of the fortress,

It is quick to cut the dwarf like grass and level life.

Before Marriage 275

— Yun

A few days ago, the Huang Mansion was really busy, and it is said that the wedding ceremony of the second young master is coming soon. His mother had carefully considered how to make the "new room" beautiful last winter, and it took a lot of effort to arrange it until now, so the second young master's new room is also decorated luxuriously.

Because Mrs. Huang's idea of hugging her grandson was too strong, she wrinkled her face with many lines, and from time to time, she showed a lot of smiles, happily discussing with her son, buying this and doing that. Sometimes it seems that she doesn't trust people, so she personally drives her own car to buy and buy. In this early spring season, the elderly are prone to illness. Mrs. Huang, who had worked a little, actually fell ill. And she was unconscious, obviously very dangerous. The maids began to take turns serving the wife day and night. According to the doctor, it was "old illness" and there was no great danger, so the second young master was relieved. But on the other hand, the sister-in-law and his elder brother regarded the mother's illness as irrelevant, of course, they didn't talk about it, or what.

Do Not Reason 276

What worries. Not only that, but they even stared at her dying, because her death would bring them tremendous benefits.

Ever since Mrs. Huang fell ill, half a month had passed, but her condition showed no improvement. The fortune teller said that the happy event of the second young master should be held earlier on an auspicious day to "counteract the ill luck," so that her illness would see the unexpected effect of resurrection from the dead without medicine.

The night was deep, and it was frighteningly quiet here, as if death

Page 18

The god had descended to the human world was so terrible!

"Mom, do you feel a little more comfortable?" The second young master comforted her in a soft voice.

"...Pain, heartache..." She sobbed.

"Your illness will get better, please be relieved, and sleep well!"

"Alas! Why don't they want to come and see me? After raising them, they don't understand filial piety. No wonder the world is going to turn upside down, and it's not like a good world! Life is uninteresting, it's better to die straightforwardly!"

"Mom, don't be angry anymore, won't you get sicker if you are like this? Don't worry, after the young daughter-in-law comes, she will definitely be filial to you."

As he spoke, he ordered the little maid A Cui to serve the lady.

The next day, a thick piece of hemp cloth was newly added to the curtain of Huang Mansion.

Store Clerk Communication

Bride Kidnapping 277

Editor:

My wife's younger sister is twenty years old this year; at the age of sixteen, she was betrothed to a farmer's son of the same age in the same village through a matchmaker, but there was no evidence. The person my wife's younger sister was betrothed to is a rogue without a job; his father is addicted to opium, and the fields and houses have all been sold. My mother-in-law and others, seeing this situation, knew that after she married, there would be no means of survival. The mother and daughter cried and came to me, asking me to rescue her from this sea of ​​misery. Seeing how pitiful they were, I had no choice but to find a way for her.

Sir, my home is in the countryside of Taicang, and my wife's younger sister

The father of the other party is very strong and unreasonable: when he heard the news, he threatened to use harsh means to kidnap the bride. I think it's not good to stay in the countryside after all, and I want to take her to Shanghai to find a job and find another partner. I will ignore the old partner.

Sir, can that old partner sue me for elopement? I respectfully ask you to choose a way out for me, and I will be very grateful. Wishing you

A bright future Hu Naiwu respectfully

X X X X

Editor's note: In various parts of our country, the procedures for engagement are mostly based on the testimony of the introducer, and there is no substantial

Physical evidence. Even in some places, a procedure of exchanging birth certificates is carried out, but because these birth certificates are not signed and sealed, they cannot be regarded as physical evidence. This custom is recognized in court; therefore, the fact that Mr. Hu's wife's younger sister is betrothed does not become ineffective because there is no evidence. Considering that she was only sixteen years old when she got engaged, she was still a minor, and of course her parents acted as agents, so this marriage contract is legally valid, but now that she is an adult, if she herself is unwilling, she can request to be dissolved. The procedure for dissolution is of course best done by agreement; in the event that both parties hold different views, then you only have to request the court to declare it, and the result is nothing more than spending some money; as long as Mr. Hu's wife's younger sister insists that she is unwilling, the court cannot force her. Ignoring it cannot be done.

Speaking of bride kidnapping, there is basically nothing to fear. Engagement is just a kind of contract, and among all kinds of contracts, its effectiveness is the smallest. Why? Because the Civil Code stipulates that no matter what, a marriage contract cannot be forcibly performed. The status of husband and wife begins only after marriage; after engagement and before marriage, the woman is still a member of her parents' family. If the fiancé seduces the fiancée, unless her parents do not pursue it, it will constitute a crime of adultery! Bride kidnapping! That's even more terrible The crime of rape cannot be escaped! But in Chinese society! Virginity is still valued, so after every bride kidnapping,

They will make the best of it, endure it, and not pursue it.

You now want to take your wife's younger sister to Shanghai to make a living, which is correct. They cannot file a lawsuit for elopement. Because your wife's younger sister is still a member of your mother-in-law's family, they are not qualified to report this crime of elopement that harms the family. However, if you want to find another marriage partner for her, then it is best to do so after her first marriage contract is declared dissolved.

Time in a Dream "Continued 39" 278

— Abandoned Lean Gull

Although the image given to him by the National University Professors' Association for National Salvation was extremely bad, he was not completely discouraged. After feeling sad at home for a few days, he was eager to try again and wanted to find another national salvation organization to participate in. Give some strength to his motherland.

"Ah! This person is a good son of the Republic of China! The support association he presides over will no longer be superficial. Go and see him!" One afternoon, Wu Yi accidentally read an amazing news item in the newspaper and couldn't help but get excited again. The gist of this news is as follows:

The escape process of Xu Songqiao, a member of the Standing Committee of the Righteous Army Support Association

"::: Mr. Xu Songqiao, a member of the Standing Committee of the Association, has always been determined to resist Japan and has spared no effort in managing the Association's affairs. They were in the process of ::: Unexpectedly, Mr. Xu suddenly escaped and returned at about three o'clock last night. According to him: ::: The guards were all from a certain country, and they were only given a basin of white rice and two or three dried radishes a day: ::: Various abuses, covered in wounds. ::: Last night, taking advantage of the guards' sleep, he escaped through the wall and ran wildly for forty or fifty miles on foot, his feet were calloused, and he was barely breathing. ::: He has now returned to his residence to recuperate and has decided to continue his work of resisting Japan and saving the country after he fully recovers. ::: If it is Mr. Xu, he is a true patriotic man of this world! :::"

Although Wu Yi had never met Xu Songqiao before and didn't know what kind of person he was, he couldn't help but feel respect after reading this passage. He deeply regretted that he hadn't read the newspaper earlier. He hurriedly inquired about the address of the Capital Righteous Army Support Association and hurried there: unexpectedly, when he looked at the place, there was a sign, and there was also a sign of a communication agency hanging on the side, but the house was already covered with the seal of the Capital Police Department, and the Iron General was guarding the door, which surprised him greatly.

But they are too radical, right? It's really unreasonable!"

Without asking right from wrong, Wu Yi spoke with a tone of blaming the Police Department for suppressing the patriotic movement.

The Xu something Qiao who was reported in the newspaper today has been arrested by our department! Fabricating rumors and defrauding money: ::: According to the charges, he will have to spend at least three years in prison!"

Li Jinbiao's words made Wu Yi even more confused.

"How about we go somewhere to drink tea and talk in detail?" Wu Yi requested this.

"I don't dare! It is Principal Suo who is treating me, so I should accompany you." As Li Jin said, he put on the air of a subordinate seeing a superior, and let Wu Yi walk in front, while he walked with his hands hanging down, one step away.

Film Special

Spring Sunshine of Palm Springs 279

— Luo Fen

A Paradise in the Soft Red Dust

Hollywood belongs to California and has a mild climate. After the severe winter gradually disappears, lovely spring follows. The snow on the mountain peaks melts, the green buds on the branches appear, and the warm spring breeze envelops the earth. This is the most vibrant time of the year in Hollywood. The stars are full of energy and work with courage.

A few miles away from the bustling area of ​​Hollywood, high mountains are connected to each other, and there is a sandy land in the mountains. On the mountainside, there is a famous spring in the United States called Palm Spring. There are very few people in winter, but when spring comes, many Hollywood figures come to Palm Spring to stroll and relax after working hard. The top of the mountain and the foot of the mountain are their world. Several famous big stars have built villas, and the entire spring is spent between the mountains and clear waters.

The big-nosed Jamie Duran, who usually pays the most attention to time economy, also holds a cigar in his hand and wears a soft hat in this lovely spring, spending a few days of uneconomical time by the Palm Spring.

Charles Leighton, after finishing "The Courtesan," felt that Hollywood was too noisy and tasteless. He was originally British, so he really wanted to go back to England. One day his friend dragged him to Palm Springs for a spring outing, and Leighton was there, and he almost thought he was no longer in Hollywood. He couldn't believe that there was such a quiet place next to such a turbid world as Hollywood. So he lived there and never mentioned going back to the country again.

Joan Crawford likes to travel alone. She drives her car to Palm Springs and lives in her villa. She wanders on the top of the mountain every day and sits on the rocks in the middle of the mountain. When it comes to dusk, she is still reluctant to leave. She said to people, "Surrounded by such scenery, any troubles in life can be put aside. Take a breath of fresh air. How can you be willing to enjoy such a peaceful blessing for a few days in a lifetime?"

Jane Gaynor doesn't care about the season. Whenever she has time from work, she immediately goes to Palm Springs to live. On average, she spends more time living in Palm Springs than in her home on Peeverly Hill. Kerr Farel is also a regular at Palm Springs, but he has now left the film industry and may become a rare visitor.

Although Palm Springs has a long history, its reputation is still due to Hollywood. In fact, the scenery near Palm Springs is not inferior to Yellowstone National Park, but everything is natural and there is no artificial mixing. Except for the El Mirador Hotel at the foot of the mountain, there are no tall buildings. Hollywood figures who are tired of living in red buildings and giant mansions naturally have infinite feelings about it.

Film Review

Review of "Red Dust" and Dog Show 280

— Si Ping

"Red Dust," which opened at Cathay yesterday, has a Chi Hen Ha Green jumping out of the darkness, but it is not as hot as before, and the wild woman is not as fierce as before. There is also a Clark Gable who never makes people happy; however, she must pretend to be a rough man, so she can't make "gentleness like water," and she can't make "passionate love like fire." It's just empty talk, the purpose is to touch the audience's subconscious. The entire plot is to move a love triangle from a familiar city to the tropical Annam, which can save a lot of scenery that needs to be capitalized. The lighting is a little worse, and the audience can be forgiven. And the unexpected benefit is that you can borrow a gust of red dust that often occurs in the tropics. Before the audience can recognize what is going on, the scene changes and the screen is calm again. A few more rain scenes make the film change from beginning to end, but during the heavy rain, a white patch is exposed in the middle of the two large dark clouds in the sky. No matter how tight the wind is blowing or how heavy the rain is, it always stays there without moving.

In the past, most of the so-called erotic and sensual films were women undressing for men to watch. In this film, it is men undressing and hinting for women to watch. This may be the highlight of the so-called "hot and wild women, happy to be violent men," right? Speaking of "violence," some places are too rough. This rough man squatted high on the tree and shot a tiger to death. Later, he gave her a pistol because of a love affair, but it seemed like a small matter like stabbing a knife. He pressed his waist and leaned slightly to the side, but did not fall to the ground. He was still able to sit on the chair and order another so-called hot and wild woman to treat this rough man. He didn't die, so his roughness was more powerful than a tiger; if he had unfortunately died of his injuries, this film would not be able to continue, and the so-called hot and wild woman would not be happy to see the rough man, and this love triangle story would not be able to reach a happy ending.

The witty remarks in "Red Dust" can embellish the entire film. Before "Red Dust" was released, there was also a short dog-made movie, which was really a dog show! However, those many dogs were dressed in a decent manner, and instead of running on all fours, they walked on two legs like humans. When the dogs opened their mouths, they were matched with human language; the audience could see the dogs' mouths opening and closing, and at the same time they could hear the words, dog mouths and human words, what a strange thing! This is really a ridiculous act that is sliding the world. Or this can also be said to be the omnipotence of science! In short, in general, the dog show is full of ugly things, making people wonder what it is saying. If it is said that in the past, Rin Tin Tin, a dog, even became a dog star, now gathering a group of dogs in one film can satisfy the audience's curiosity, then this kind of curiosity is really unacceptable.

Ancient Country Beauty The Mummy 281

— Yan Nan

The ancient country beauty Mummy, which was re-screened at Carlton the day before yesterday, is a supernatural film. The stories of supernatural films are always bizarre, so I will record them in more detail below.

In 1922, British archaeologists in Egypt found a mummy, but because they were careless, they opened an ancient incantation, so the mummy was resurrected and took the curse away. In 1932, other archaeologists planned to make some discoveries. At that time, the mummy ran to the garrison and pointed out the tomb of a certain Egyptian princess 3,700 years ago, which was indeed excavated and displayed in the British Museum in Egypt. The mummy recited a curse to the corpse and knew that the princess had been reincarnated in this world as an Egyptian noblewoman. The mummy tried its best to seize her for itself and told a love story that had not been completed 3,700 years ago.

, planning to die with her to seek spiritual union. However, there was a young archaeologist whose father died at the hands of the mummy, and he also deeply loved the girl, so he secretly became enemies with the mummy, but the mummy was so powerful that it could know the past and the future, and could control people from thousands of miles away. Although the archaeologist went to the mummy's house and witnessed the mummy trying to kill the girl, he could not help. In a critical moment, the idol enshrined in the mummy's house suddenly emitted golden light, which not only boosted the archaeologist's spirit and made him unafraid of magic, but also turned the mummy into a rotting corpse, and its body was shattered into pieces, so the girl was unharmed. The screenwriter's purpose is to be extremely mysterious, to make the audience feel terror and tension, so it is completely detached from reality and becomes an absurd fantasy. Reason is of course out of the question, but the ending with evil not invading good is very clever and commendable.

Structurally, the entire film is very compact, consistent from beginning to end, and the terrifying places come one after another. Not only are "Desert Island Monster" and "Terror Grotto" far inferior to this film, but even the supernatural masterpiece "Frankenstein" is inferior to it. The artistic success is above all horror films.

The director is also not bad. With a good plot and actors, although the director does not spend much effort, his ability is not weak during the performance. Some trivial small shots and secret writings are very vivid. Many scenes that seem to be finished but not finished not only do not feel disconnected, but also have lingering charm to be found. The photography is also very beautiful. is a capable hand. The scenery has the ancient Egyptian style. The lighting and sound are also on par with the photography: : : In short, there are no loopholes to be found in terms of technology.

Finally, I will talk about the vivid actors in this film: 克洛夫 Boris Karloff is famous for his supernatural films. His slow movements are very suitable for the identity of the mummy. The meticulous makeup is also something that others cannot imitate. Last time, his performance as a zombie was banned because it was too bizarre, which was generally regretted. This time, he is still such a supernatural character, and we can actually see it, which is really the fate of the film, and it is fortunate and unfortunate! The girl is played by 琪塔裘汉 Zita Johann, who has the typical Egyptian beauty of the past, and the performance is also top-notch. In addition, there is an archaeologist who is frightened and goes crazy because the mummy is resurrected, and laughs wildly because he is crazy, which is extremely profound. The other supporting roles are much worse.

In short, its beauty is indescribable, especially the scene where the mummy tells the old story of three thousand years ago, which is fascinating. So this film can be said to be satisfactory to anyone!

Raw Materials for Making Up Mummies 282

— Luo Fen

Universal Company's latest blockbuster "Ancient Country Beauty"

The Mummy (original translation: Mummy) is a great historical film. The story in it is about the ancient Egyptian celebrities who died and were smeared with spices to make them permanently incorruptible, as well as various stories about mummies that have been passed down in history. The protagonist who plays the mummy is 保里斯卡洛夫, the monster in "Frankenstein". In this "Ancient Country Beauty", he uses various makeup techniques to transform himself into a thin and small mummy with a pigeon-shaped face, making his body shrink. This is a very difficult thing.

The mummy played by 保里斯卡洛夫 is said to be 3,700 years old. When 保里斯 is making up, he wets his face with water, then applies a very thin layer of cotton on his face, then applies collodion "fake ivory solution" and a layer of alcohol resin to make the collodion shrink. After the body is tightly tied with bandages, resin is applied, and the hands and feet are tightly tied with rubber paste bandages. After the chest is tightly tied, it is extremely difficult to breathe, but 保里斯 can endure the work, each time for up to five hours. In the last scene, 保里斯 extended it to eight hours. 保里斯 is one of the only people after the thousand-faced man 郎 却奈 died. Although Hollywood is big, there is no second person who is willing to sacrifice his life for art.

Tom Mix's Past 283

— Dong Lin

Participated in the Eight-Power Allied Forces

Not long ago, someone in this publication wrote an article to lament the retirement of Tom Mix. This kind of thing is completely unnecessary. I wonder if Mr. has heard about Tom Mix's life?

Before Tom Mix entered the screen, he was a junior officer in the American army. When the Eight-Power Allied Forces attacked Beijing in 1899, he also participated in this battle; at that time, it was said that he had killed countless Chinese people. After the war ended, he was discharged from the army due to serious injuries. Although the Boxer Rebellion was a disaster brewed by the Qing Dynasty itself, the people who killed our compatriots are always our enemies. Then what are we still lamenting for Tom's retirement?

Editor's note: Although Mr. Donglin's opinion comes from patriotic feelings, there are also errors. In times of war, it is useless and harmful to pursue former grudges or resent a certain individual who participated in the war without being able to kill the enemy and achieve results, because in this case, wouldn't everyone in the world be our enemy?

Motion Picture Novel: Cavalcade "10" 284

— Ne

Kee Yin was now extremely heartbroken, she couldn't imagine how Ellen, such a loyal servant, could treat her former mistress with such disrespect. So she said, "Yes, this world has changed too strangely. Ellen, you've changed too, your heart is no longer what it used to be. Ellen, farewell." Ellen, hearing this, became uncontrollably furious, she said: "Why are you still putting on airs and trying to drive me away?"

Just as they were arguing more and more fiercely, a maid brought in a telegram. Kee Yin took the telegram, opened it, and read it. She said to Ellen: "You don't need to worry about Fannie Joey anymore. He won't be coming back either. He's dead!"

Ellen quickly stepped forward and supported Kee Yin. Kee Yin fainted and fell into Ellen's arms, the telegram falling to the ground. Ellen shouted: "Madam! My Madam!" Only then did Ellen recover her true nature, and she was once again a loyal servant to her mistress.

After the armistice, London inevitably had celebrations. Kee Yin wandered alone in the streets, trying to find her son Joey among the crowd to guide him home. In the midst of the honking horns and clanging bells of celebration, crowds sang and danced in the streets, and sometimes she was grabbed by ignorant celebrants and pulled into the dancing. She listlessly returned home, having not found her son, with many red, green and colorful paper strips wrapped around her hat and throat. She vaguely recalled that there had been a similar celebration many years ago, probably when Mafeking in South Africa was relieved!

The war was over, and everything had changed, unbelievably changed! The tide of sin rose day by day; the people wanted to forget the pain of the war and engaged in indulgence and extravagance; thus there were nightclubs, male dance partners, robbers, kidnappers, etc., and even children playing in the streets were sprayed with machine guns! These were even more terrible than war. And there were the divorce cases that were reported in the newspapers every day. Peace was getting further and further away! Countries continued to argue incessantly; the League of Nations was like an empty dream; unemployment, hunger, and riots filled the British Isles.

Thus it was the end of another year. Robert raised his glass towards Kee Yin and said: "Another year has passed!" Kee Yin couldn't help but shudder. She said: "Another year is before us!" The distant bells rang again; the streets were filled with boisterous people, singing the tune of Auld Lang Syne, a tune that broke Kee Yin's heart. She stood beside her husband and said: "All the glory and victory have become things of the past; all the sorrow and bitterness have become like the joys and sorrows in a dream. Let us now drink a glass of wine, firstly to commemorate our two sons who sacrificed themselves for the country; and secondly to commemorate the fact that our own hearts have died with them!" As they drank, they saw groups of figures, like fleeting clouds, dazzling before their eyes; these past figures were all part of their lives 丨 Bridges and Ellen raised their glasses to celebrate the arrival of the new century; the children stood beside them in their pajamas, with astonished eyes; Edith and Edward looked at each other and smiled, their love endless; Joey's childishness would never grow up; Margaret's spirit of courage and progress; Fannie, the only flower in London, but her heart would always have Joey 丨丨 Robert and Kee Yin still looked at each other and smiled, still with hope, heading forward until the end of the world. "The End"
